        <h1>Will his rivals put the boot in? Jeb Bush wears shoe held together with sticky tape during campaign town hall meeting </h1>
<ul class="mol-bullets-with-font"><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>The Republican candidate wore the old shoes in Nashua, New Hampshire</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Bush ran an ad that poked fun at the  cowboy boots worn by  Rubio</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong><a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" href="/news/prince_charles/index.html">Prince Charles</a> famously wears old Lobb shoes that cost thousands </strong></font></li></ul><p class="author-section byline-plain">By

<a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Ted+Thornhill+for+MailOnline" class="author" rel="nofollow">Ted Thornhill for MailOnline</a>


</p>
<p class="byline-section"><span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-published">
  <span class="article-timestamp-label">Published:</span>
  09:06 EST, 8 February 2016
</span>
 | <span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-updated">

  15:40 EST, 8 February 2016
</span>

</p><div itemprop="articleBody"><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em"><a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" href="/news/jeb_bush/index.html">Jeb Bush</a> recently pointed out that he doesn't need big cowboy boots like the sort Marco Rubio wears, because he's already tall enough.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">But it seems he does need a new pair of shoes of some variety, because he was photographed wearing one that was taped up at the side.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">An eagle-eyed photographer snapped the scruffy shoe while the former Florida governor and Republican candidate attended a campaign town hall meeting in Nashua, New Hampshire, on Sunday.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em"><span class="mol-style-bold">Scroll down for video </span></font></p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img">  <img id="i-b051debdeb8c31ba" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/08/13/30FCB2F800000578-0-image-a-19_1454939396622.jpg" height="422" width="634" alt="A piece of tape holds together U.S. Republican presidential candidate Jeb Bush's shoe during a campaign town hall meeting in Nashua, New Hampshire" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div>    <p class="imageCaption">A piece of tape holds together U.S. Republican presidential candidate Jeb Bush's shoe during a campaign town hall meeting in Nashua, New Hampshire</p></div><div class="mol-img-group floatRHS">    <div class="mol-img">  <img id="i-dd81ec260dc9a518" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/08/15/30FF048100000578-3437211-Prince_Charles_has_famously_attended_public_gatherings_wearing_d-a-32_1454944428865.jpg" height="706" width="306" alt="Prince Charles has famously attended public gatherings wearing decades-old Lobb shoes, which cost thousands of dollars" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div>    <p class="imageCaption">Prince Charles has famously attended public gatherings wearing decades-old Lobb shoes, which cost thousands of dollars</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">However, some may argue that when it comes to sporting well-worn footwear, Mr Bush is in good company.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Prince Charles has famously attended public gatherings wearing decades-old Lobb shoes, which cost thousands of dollars.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Last month 6ft 3in Bush ran a Super PAC ad that poked fun at the chunky cowboy boots worn by Republican challenger Marco Rubio.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">And when MSNBC Morning Joe host Joe Scarborough told him that some say 5ft 10in Rubio wears the boots to boost his height, he replied that he 'doesn't have a height issue'.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Hopefuls Bush and Chris Christie say Rubio hasn't been tested in a way that the governors running for president have, leaving him unqualified to be president.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Bush referred to Rubio as 'a bright, charismatic leader' on MSNBC, but described his leadership skills as a 'work in progress.'</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Christie, New Jersey's sitting governor, repeated accusations that Rubio recites the same campaign points, calling him a 'talented guy' when required to 'deliver a speech, read a teleprompter.'</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Bush also attacked billionaire Donald Trump, with whom he clashed at Saturday's GOP debate over the issue of eminent domain, calling him a 'loser.'</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">The debate on Saturday had begun in chaos as several candidates didn't come on stage as ABC News moderators David Muir and Martha Raddatz called their names.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Dr. Ben Carson came to the mouth of a backstage hallway at St. Anselm College too early, as his name was to be the second called. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">With applause ringing through the hall for Chris Christie, he never heard his name.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Carson stopped just short of entering and was stranded in no-man's land and in view of a TV camera trained on the entryway.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em"> </font></p><div><div class="related-carousel with-fb news"
     id="p-18"
     data-track-module="am-related_carousel^related_carousel" data-track-selector=".rotator-panels a:not([class*=external])" data-track-pos="static">

     data-track-module="am-infinite_list^infinite_list" data-track-selector="h3 a" data-track-pos="static">
  <h2 class="wocc">More top stories</h2>

<script async src="//cdn.taboola.com/libtrc/dailymail-us/loader.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = 10;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '<div id="' + id + '" style="min-height: 280px;"></div>';
            $(node).before(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n});
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=news&pageSize=10',
            total: 22.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
</script>
